***freaky.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:freaky.html>freaky</a> (42315)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:freak.html>freak</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">-y</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:freaky.html>freaky</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en comparative-form-of" lang="en">freakier</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en superlative-form-of" lang="en">freakiest</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Resembling a <a href = vnd.unilang:freak.html>freak</a>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Odd; bizarre; unusual.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">I've <a href = vnd.unilang:heard.html>heard</a> the props and costumes in this play are quite <b><a href = vnd.unilang:freaky.html>freaky</a></b>.</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Scary; frightening.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">Have you <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:freaky.html>freaky</a></b> new guy who moved in next <a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a>?</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Sexually deviant.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">The <a href = vnd.unilang:things.html>things</a> she asked <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> to do <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> too <b><a href = vnd.unilang:freaky.html>freaky</a></b> for <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a>.</i></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
</body>

***fregat.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:fregat.html>fregat</a> (32664)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">frégate</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">fregata</i>, cognate with Spanish amp; Portuguese <i class="Latn mention" lang="pt">fragata</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:fregat.html>fregat</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:fregatten.html>fregatten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:fregat.html>fregatje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A frigate, a type of (once sailing, small but fast three-mast) warship, applied to progressively larger <a href = vnd.unilang:types.html>types</a> in time, since 1943 mainly escort ships.</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:fregat.html>fregat</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic"><a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>o</a></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:scheepvaart.html>scheepvaart</a>)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:oorlogsschip.html>oorlogsschip</a></li>

***fresco.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:fresco.html>fresco</a> (75959)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it"><a href = vnd.unilang:fresco.html>fresco</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Medieval_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Medieval Latin">Medieval Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">friscus</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*friskaz</i>, whence also <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vers.html>vers</a></i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:fris.html>fris</a></i>.
</p>

***friemelen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:friemelen.html>friemelen</a> (39572)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps a variant of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:frommelen.html>frommelen</a></i>, through influence of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wriemelen.html>wriemelen</a></i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">friemeln</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">fumble</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Icelandic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Icelandic language">Icelandic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="is">fálma</i>. 
</p>

***fries.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:fries.html>fries</a> (57521)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">frise</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:fries.html>fries</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> or <abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:friezen.html>friezen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:fries.html>friesje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:fris.html>fris</a> (4315)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From late <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">frisch</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">vrisch</i>, borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">vrisch</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">frisc</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*frisk</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*friskaz</i>. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vers.html>vers</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***frituur.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:frituur.html>frituur</a> (32663)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm"><a href = vnd.unilang:frituren.html>friture</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">frīctūra</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">frīctūrus</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:frituur.html>frituur</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:frituren.html>frituren</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:frituur.html>frituurtje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>) <span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belgium" class="extiw" title="w:Belgium">Belgium</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span>
</p>
<ol><li>Deep-fried food, now especially used of <a href = vnd.unilang:snacks.html>snacks</a> and fast food. <span class="defdate">[from 16th c.]</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>We</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:eten.html>eten</a> morgenochtend <b><a href = vnd.unilang:frituur.html>frituur</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>We</a> will eat <b>deep-fried fastfood</b> tomorrow morning.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>A chip shop, a friterie, a fast food takeaway selling deep-fried food. <span class="defdate">[from 20th c.]</span></li></ol>

</p>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">frietkot</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">Belgium</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>

***frons.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:frons.html>frons</a> (43781)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">fronce</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">fronce</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Frankish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Frankish language">Frankish</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*hrunkja</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">wrinkle</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hrunkijō</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hrunkitō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fold, wrinkle</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*sker-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to turn, bend</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The semantic narrowing to frowns on the forehead may be influenced by unrelated <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">frōns</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:frons.html>frons</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:fronsen.html>fronsen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:fronsje.html>fronsje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A frown, a furrow of one's eyebrows or forehead.</li></ol>

***frosty.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:frosty.html>frosty</a> (19660)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:frosty.html>frosty</a></i>; equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">frost</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">-y</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:frosty.html>frosty</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en comparative-form-of" lang="en">frostier</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en superlative-form-of" lang="en">frostiest</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Cold, chilly.
<dl><dd><i>The air <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:frosty.html>frosty</a></b>; I could see my breath and walked quickly with my hands in my <a href = vnd.unilang:pockets.html>pockets</a>.</i></dd>
<dd><i>I'd like a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:frosty.html>frosty</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:milkshake.html>milkshake</a>.</i></dd></dl></li>
<li>Having frost on it.
<dl><dd><i>The <b><a href = vnd.unilang:frosty.html>frosty</a></b> pumpkin <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> the sign of the end of the growing season, soon the greenery will wither and harvest end for the year.</i></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Having an aloof or inhospitable manner.
<dl><dd><i>After the divorce, she <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> civil but <b><a href = vnd.unilang:frosty.html>frosty</a></b> to her <a href = vnd.unilang:ex.html>ex</a>.</i></dd></dl></li></ol>
</body>

***fuik.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:fuik.html>fuik</a> (70057)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">fuke</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">fyke</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:fuik.html>fuik</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:fuiken.html>fuiken</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:fuik.html>fuikje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">fyke</span></li></ol>

***fulcrum.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:fulcrum.html>fulcrum</a> (45502)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:fulcrum.html>fulcrum</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bedpost, foot of a couch</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">fulciō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">prop up, support</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:fulcrum.html>fulcrum</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">fulcrums</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">fulcra</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:mechanics.html>mechanics</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The support about which a <a href = vnd.unilang:lever.html>lever</a> pivots.
<dl><dd><i>It <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> possible to flick food across the table using your fork as a <a href = vnd.unilang:lever.html>lever</a> and your finger as a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:fulcrum.html>fulcrum</a></b>.</i></dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>2010</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/John_Allison_(artist)" class="extiw" title="w:John Allison (artist)">John Allison</a>, <i><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://scarygoround.com/?date=20100126">Bad Machinery</a></i>
<dl><dd>MILDRED: Archimedes <a href = vnd.unilang:said.html>said</a> give <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> a <a href = vnd.unilang:lever.html>lever</a> long enough and a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:fulcrum.html>fulcrum</a></b> on which to place it and I will move the world.</dd>
<dd><a href = vnd.unilang:charlotte.html>Charlotte</a>: Yeah she <a href = vnd.unilang:said.html>said</a> that twaddle eight or nine times.</dd></dl></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2012</b> March 1,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Henry_Petroski" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Henry Petroski"><a href = vnd.unilang:henry.html>Henry</a> Petroski</a>,  “Opening Doors”, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/American_Scientist" class="extiw" title="w:American Scientist">American Scientist</a></cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.americanscientist.org/issues/pub/opening-doors">[1]</a></sup>, volume 100, number 2, page 112-3:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">A doorknob of whatever roundish shape <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> effectively a continuum of <a href = vnd.unilang:levers.html>levers</a>, with the axis of the latching mechanism | known as the spindle | being the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:fulcrum.html>fulcrum</a></b> about which the turning <a href = vnd.unilang:takes.html>takes</a> place.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A crux or pivot; a central point.
<ul><li><b>2006</b>, Rebecca Langlands, <i>Sexual Morality in Ancient <a href = vnd.unilang:rome.html>Rome</a></i> (page 119)
<dl><dd>By this point the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:fulcrum.html>fulcrum</a></b> of concern <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> the <i>stuprum</i> of <a href = vnd.unilang:men.html>men</a> upon <a href = vnd.unilang:men.html>men</a>, described as more <a href = vnd.unilang:prevalent.html>prevalent</a> than that upon women.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
</body>

***fuller.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:fuller.html>fuller</a> (9733)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">full</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:fuller.html>fuller</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">comparative form of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">full</i></span></span>: more <span class="Latn" lang="en">full</span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">full</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i>, from the verb.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:fuller.html>fuller</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:fullers.html>fullers</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A person who fulls cloth.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">walker</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">waulker</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/10/Cawood_sword_-_guard_-_YORYM_2007_3086.JPG/220px-Cawood_sword_-_guard_-_YORYM_2007_3086.JPG" decoding="async" width="220" height="165" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/10/Cawood_sword_-_guard_-_YORYM_2007_3086.JPG/330px-Cawood_sword_-_guard_-_YORYM_2007_3086.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/10/Cawood_sword_-_guard_-_YORYM_2007_3086.JPG/440px-Cawood_sword_-_guard_-_YORYM_2007_3086.JPG 2x" data-file-width="1280" data-file-height="960" />  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"></div>Sword blade with <a href = vnd.unilang:fuller.html>fuller</a> along the centre.</div></div></div>
<p>Unknown origin.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:fuller.html>fuller</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:fullers.html>fullers</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A convex, rounded or grooved tool, used by blacksmiths for shaping metal.</li>
<li>A groove made by such a tool (in the blade of a sword etc.).</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:fuller.html>fuller</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:fullers.html>fullers</a></b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">fullering</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">fullered</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To form a groove or channel in, by a <a href = vnd.unilang:fuller.html>fuller</a> or set hammer.
<dl><dd><i>to <b><a href = vnd.unilang:fuller.html>fuller</a></b> a bayonet</i></dd></dl></li></ol>
